		<Float Name="BulkUpstreamRxTimeout">
			<ToolTip>Sets the Bulk upstream receive timeout counter.</ToolTip>
			<Description>Sets the Bulk upstream receive timeout counter. The timeout counter is also set to this value when a byte is written to or pulled off the Bulk upstream FIFO. When different than 0, the counter decrements by one every system clock cycle until it reaches 0. Bytes present in the FIFO are delivered to the application when the timeout occurs.</Description>
			<DisplayName>Upstream Receive Timeout</DisplayName>

		<Boolean Name="ClSafePowerActive">
			<ToolTip>Controls whether the SafePower protocol is active.</ToolTip>
			<Description>Controls whether the SafePower protocol is active. SafePower is a protocol to prevent the Video Interface from attempting to supply power to a conventional (non PoCL) cable or camera. When set to True, SafePower is enabled on the Video Interface. When set to False, SafePower is disabled i.e. the Video Interface behaves like in a conventional Camera Link system. In this case, the Video Interface does not attempt to supply power to a Camera Link connector/camera pair for the selected Camera Link interface. The inner shield lines of the associated Camera Link connector are tied to digital ground in the Video Interface.</Description>
			<DisplayName>CL SafePower Active</DisplayName>
			<Visibility>Expert</Visibility>
			<Streamable>Yes</Streamable>
			<pValue>ClSafePowerActiveReg</pValue>

		<Enumeration Name="ClSafePowerStatus">
			<ToolTip>Reports the status of the SafePower controller.</ToolTip>
			<Description>Reports the status of the SafePower controller. When set to Initializing, PoCL camera and cable detection has not started yet. When set to PoClSensing, the controller senses if a PoCL camera and cable are connected. When set to PoClCameraAndCableDetected, the controller detected a PoCL camera and cable but the presence of a clock has not been detected yet. When set to PoClLinkUp, a clock has been detected on a PoCL camera and cable pair. When set to NonPoClCameraOrCableDetected, the controller detected a non-PoCL camera or cable but the presence of a clock has not been detected yet. When set to NonPoClLinkUp, a clock has been detected on a non-PoCL camera and cable pair. In normal operation with a connected camera, this feature should report PoClLinkUp or NonPoClLinkUp.</Description>
			<DisplayName>CL SafePower Status</DisplayName>
